# Apple Inc. (AAPL) — Financial Statements

> Source: Apple Inc. SEC 10-K / 10-Q filings, Apple Investor Relations (investor.apple.com)
> All figures in USD millions ($M) unless noted. Market Cap in USD billions ($B).
> Apple fiscal year ends in late September. Q1=Oct-Dec, Q2=Jan-Mar, Q3=Apr-Jun, Q4=Jul-Sep.
> FY2025 Q3/Q4 and FY2026 Q1 figures are estimates based on public earnings guidance and analyst consensus.
